 1961 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      1 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | *-------------------------------------------------
 1962 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      2 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | * Create_Sprite — Compiled sprite engine
 1963 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      3 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | * Ported from FTA's CREATE.SPRITE.S (1989)
 1964 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      4 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | *
 1965 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
 1966 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
 1967 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | *
 1968 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
 1969 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
 1970 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0D18               | *
